<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:binden.html>binden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bindan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bindaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰendʰ-</i>.
</p>

***binnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a> (181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*binnan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>inside, indoors
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regent.html>regent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>When it <a href = vnd.unilang:rains.html>rains</a> it's better to stay <b>inside</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (to) inside, into
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schip.html>schip</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voerde.html>voerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haven.html>haven</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a></b>.</i>

***binnengaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:binnengaan.html>binnengaan</a> (9654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inside</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">walk, go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnengaan.html>binnengaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enter, go into (a room, etc.)</li>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i>. Perhaps backformed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnenlands.html>binnenlands</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>everything within the boundaries of a nation (as opposed to <a href = vnd.unilang:buitenland.html>buitenland</a>)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b>binnenlandpagina</b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krant.html>krant</a></i>: the national news section in the newspaper</dd></dl></li>
<li>inland</li></ol>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnenvallen.html>binnenvallen</a></i>. ***biologie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:biologie.html>biologie</a> (8904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:biologie.html>Biologie</a></i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βιολογία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">biología</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a compound of <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βίος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bíos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λόγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lógos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reason</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the suffix <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">-ία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (forms abstracta), equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bio-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-logie</i>.

***bioloog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bioloog.html>bioloog</a> (17395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:biologe.html>Biologe</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">biologue</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bio-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loog</i>.

***bionic.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>bionic</a> (61620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Blend of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bio-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">electronic</i>. The <i>superhuman</i> sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attributed to the <a href = vnd.unilang:tv.html>Tv</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Six_Million_Dollar_Man" class="extiw" title="w:The Six Million Dollar Man">The Six Million <a href = vnd.unilang:dollar.html>Dollar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Bionic_Woman" class="extiw" title="w:The Bionic Woman">The <a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>Bionic</a> Woman</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>bionic</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>bionic</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>bionic</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">not comparable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Related to <a href = vnd.unilang:bionics.html>bionics</a>.</li>
<li>Of a biological organism, having <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> enhanced by electronic or mechanical parts; <a href = vnd.unilang:cyborg.html>cyborg</a>.</li>
<li>Superhuman
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Yasmin <a href = vnd.unilang:shiraz.html>Shiraz</a>,  <cite>The Blueprint for My <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>Girls</a>: How to Build a Life Full of Courage, ...</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?isbn=1416587381">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Entering womanhood <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> awesome, but the learning, growing, and obstacle facing are not going to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a>. As you grow into womanhood, it's going to seem as if the world wants you to be <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>bionic</a></b> | be stronger, faster, and smarter.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> January 21,  Virginia Heffernan,  “Trump's jargon <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> infectious”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>Los</a> Angeles Times</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But to hear the presidential physician tell it, Trump <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>bionic</a></b>. In a news conference, Rear Adm. Ronny Jackson hailed Trump's health as  "excellent" eight times.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> July 20,  <a href = vnd.unilang:lisa.html>Lisa</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Carroll,  “Ireland open to new proposal on Brexit border”, in  <cite>The Guardian</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Before leaving the factory, May <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> Delma Käthner, a local woman, who <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> her she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> “<b><a href = vnd.unilang:bionic.html>bionic</a></b>”. / “She’s coped with so much,” Käthner <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>. “She <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a terrible job. Just look at the way her <a href = vnd.unilang:shoulders.html>shoulders</a> are hunched. She <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the whole weight of Brexit on her.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***bioscoop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bioscoop.html>bioscoop</a> (4527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bioscope</i> and/or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bioscop</i> (now <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bioskop</i>), a term used in the names of two early <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> projectors, developed by the Frenchman <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georges_Demen%C3%BF" class="extiw" title="w:Georges Demenÿ">Georges Demenÿ</a> and the German <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Skladanowsky" class="extiw" title="w:Max Skladanowsky"><a href = vnd.unilang:max.html>Max</a> Skladanowsky</a>, respectively. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bioscope</i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βίος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bíos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bio-, life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σκοπέω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skopéō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I look at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus roughly “watching life”. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bio-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-scoop</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>cinema; movie <a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bios.html>bios</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">cinema</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:filmzaal.html>filmzaal</a></span></span></dd></dl>

***bisschop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bisschop.html>bisschop</a> (4773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bischop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">biskop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">episcopus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐπίσκοπος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">epískopos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The use of the term for mulled wine probably derived from English or German.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bisschop.html>bisschop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bisschoppen.html>bisschoppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bisschop.html>bisschopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bishop</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">bishop's wine</span> <span class="defdate">[from late 18th c.]</span></li></ol>

***bist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bist.html>bist</a> (95120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:bist.html>bist</a></i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bes.html>bes</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, dialectal English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bist.html>bist</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beest.html>beest</a></i>.
</p><p>German <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bist.html>bist</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> two sources:
</p>
<ul><li>a form based on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁ésti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(you) are (sg.)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>an initial <i>b-</i> that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> added to the word under influence of verb forms based on Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*beuną</i> (as in Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">beon</i>)<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<dl><dd><i>Du <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bist.html>bist</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nicht.html>nicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mein.html>mein</a> Sohn.</i>
<dl><dd>You are not my son.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Attested from c. 1920, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:bistro.html>bistro</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>)</i> with the original meaning "proprietor of a tavern" (1880s), of unknown origin, presumably regional French dialect.

***bitterzoet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bitterzoet.html>bitterzoet</a> (54950)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bitter</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zoet.html>zoet</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bitterzoet.html>bitterzoet</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bitterzoet.html>bitterzoeter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bitterzoetst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bittersweet</span>, simultaneously sweet and bitter</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bittersweet</span>, evoking or involving both sad and pleasant emotions</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bitterzoet.html>bitterzoet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="gender incomplete">?</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <small>[please provide]</small>, <i>diminutive</i> <small>[please provide]</small>)
</p>
